################################
# Atlantik Wall
################################
event = {
	id = 1300000
	random = no
	country = GER

	decision = { 
		war = { country = GER country = ENG } 
		war = { country = GER country = SOV } 
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = FRA } }
		OR = { 
			control = { province = 37 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 39 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 44 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 46 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 49 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 51 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 53 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 68 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 69 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 114 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 115 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 122 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 125 data = GER } 
		}
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		money = 3000
		metal = 20000
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			ai = no
			AND = {
				money = 3000
				metal = 20000
			}
		}
		war = { country = GER country = ENG } 
		war = { country = GER country = SOV } 
		NOT = { war = { country = GER country = FRA } }
		OR = { 
			control = { province = 37 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 39 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 44 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 46 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 49 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 51 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 53 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 68 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 69 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 114 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 115 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 122 data = GER } 
			control = { province = 125 data = GER } 
		}
	}
   
	name = "1300001name"
	desc = "1300001desc" 
	style = 2
	picture = "Wehrmacht"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1914 }
	offset = 15
	deathdate = { day = 30 month = december year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = "1300001text"
		command = { type = building_prod_mod which = coastal_fort value = 50 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = money value = -3000 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = metalpool value = -20000 }
		command = { type = industrial_modifier which = total value = 2 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 1300001 }
	}
}
event = {
	id = 1300001
	random = no
	country = FRA

	name = "1300001name"
	desc = "1300001desc" 
	style = 2
	picture = "Wehrmacht"

	action = {
		name = ACTION_NAME_OK
		command = { type = industrial_modifier which = total value = 2 }
		command = { type = dissent value = -3 }
		command = { type = domestic which = defense_lobby value = 1 }
	}
}
################################
# Grand Offensive - GER
################################
event = {
	id = 1300002
	random = no
	country = GER
	
	decision = { atwar = yes }

	decision_trigger = { supplies = 20000 }

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			ai = yes
			supplies = 20000
		}
		OR = {
			war = { country = GER country = SOV }
			lost_national = { country = GER value = 10 }
		}
	}

	name = "GrandOffensiveName"
	desc = "GrandOffensiveDesc" 
	style = 2
	picture = "Wehrmacht"
	decision_picture = "decision_grand_offensive"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1914 }
	offset = 10
	deathdate = { day = 30 month = december year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = "GrandOffensiveText"
		command = { type = max_organization which = land value = 10 }
		command = { type = morale which = land value = 10 }
		command = { type = morale which = naval value = 10 }
		command = { type = morale which = air value = 10 }
		command = { type = counterattack value = 2 }
		command = { type = assault value = 2 }
		command = { type = ambush value = 2 }
		command = { type = breakthrough value = 2 }
		command = { type = encirclement value = 2 }
		command = { type = hq_supply_eff value = 2 }
		command = { type = sce_frequency value = 0.3 }
		command = { type = attrition_mod value = 2 }
		command = { type = trickleback_mod value = 5 }
		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = supplies value = -20000 }
		command = { type = event which = 1300003 where = -1 when = 30 }
	}
}

		OR = { 
			ai = yes
			supplies = 20000
		}
		OR = {
			lost_national = { country = SOV value = 30 }
			AND = { 
				war = { country = GER country = SOV } 
				lost_national = { country = GER value = 10 } 
			}
		}
	}
   
	name = "GrandOffensiveName"
	desc = "GrandOffensiveDesc" 
	style = 2
	picture = "Wehrmacht"

		command = { type = morale which = naval value = 10 }
		command = { type = morale which = air value = 10 }
		command = { type = counterattack value = 2 }
		command = { type = assault value = 2 }
		command = { type = ambush value = 2 }
		command = { type = breakthrough value = 2 }
		command = { type = encirclement value = 2 }

		command = { trigger = { ai = no } type = supplies value = -20000 }
		command = { type = event which = 1300005 where = -1 when = 30 }

event = {
	id = 9000021
	random = no
	persistent = yes
	TAG =  { AFG ALB ALG ANG ARA ARG ARM AST AUS AZB BEL BEN BLR BOL BOS BRA BRU BUL BUR CAL CAM CAN CGX CHC CHI CHL CMB COL CON COS CRO CSA CSX CUB CXB CYN CYP CZE DDR DEN DFR EAF ECU EGY ENG EQA EST ETH EUS FIN FLA FRA GAB GEO GER GLD GRE GUA GUI GUY HOL HON HUN ICL IDC IND INO IRE IRQ ISR ITA JAP JOR KAZ KOR KUR KYG LAO LAT LBY LEB LIT LUX MAD MAL MAN MEN MEX MLY MON MOR MOZ MTN NAM NIC NIG NOR NZL OMN OTT PAK PAL PAN PAR PER PHI POL POR PRI PRK PRU QUE RHO ROM RSI RUS SAF SAL SAR SAU SCA SCH SCO SER SIA SIB SIE SIK SLO SLV SOM SOV SPA SPR SUD SWE SYR TAJ TAN TEX TRA TRK TUN TUR UKR URU USA UZB VEN VIE WLL YEM YUG U01 U02 U03 U04 U08 U09 U10 U11 U12 U13 U14 U15 U16 U17 U18 U19 U20 U21 U22 U26 U27 U28 U29 U30 U31 U32 U33 U34 U35 U40 U41 U42 U43 U44 U45 U46 U47 U48 U49 U50 U51 U52 U53 U54 U55 U56 U57 U58 U59 U67 UTC UER UPE U70 U71 U72 U73 U74 U75 U76 U77 U78 U79 U80 U81 U82 U83 U84 U85 U86 U87 U88 U89 U90 U91 U92 U93 U94 U95 U96 U97 U98 U99 }
	decision = { 
		OR = {
			money = 3000
			AND = {
				NOT = { IC = 80 }
				money = 2000
				}
			AND = {
				NOT = { IC = 50 }
				money = 1500
				}
			AND = {
				NOT = { IC = 15 }
				money = 500
				}	
			}
		OR = { 
			NOT = { policy = { type = free_market value = 8 } }
			headofstate = 240001 # FDR
		}
	}

	decision_trigger = {
		OR = {
			money = 6000
			AND = {
				NOT = { IC = 80 }
				money = 4000
				}
			AND = {
				NOT = { IC = 50 }
				money = 3000
				}
			AND = {
				NOT = { IC = 15 }
				money = 1000
				}	
			}
		atwar = no
	}

	trigger = {
		money = 6000
		OR = { 
			NOT = { policy = { type = free_market value = 8 } }
			headofstate = 240001 # FDR
		}
	}
   
	name = "9000021name"
	desc = "9000021desc" 
	style = 2
	picture = "public_jobs"
	decision_picture = "decision_public_jobs"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1914 }
	offset = 120
	deathdate = { day = 30 month = december year = 1963 }

	action = {
		name = "9000021text"
		command = { type = dissent value = -2 }
		command = { trigger = { IC = 80 } type = money value = -6000 }

				money = 250

				}	
			}
	}

		OR = {
			random = 80
			dissent = 3
		}
		government = democratic
		atwar = yes
		money = 500
	}

		command = { type = local_setflag which = press_censorship }
	}
